Black Opium was created by Nathalie Lorson, Marie Salamagne, Olivier Cresp and Honorine Blanc. Top notes are Pear, Pink Pepper and Orange Blossom; middle notes are Coffee, Jasmine, Bitter Almond and Licorice; base notes are Vanilla, Patchouli, Cashmere Wood and Cedar. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>In September of 2014 Yves Saint Laurent launches Black Opium, the new fragrance announced as a rock'n'roll interpretation of the classic that should highlight the dark, mysterious side of the YSL brand. Master perfumers Nathalie Lorson and Marie Salamagne, in collaboration with Olivier Cresp and Honorine Blanc, developed the composition. Notes of coffee, present in large quantities, dominate the scent. Additional accords are pink pepper, orange blossom, jasmine, vanilla, patchouli and cedar.
</p>

<p>
The perfume comes in the bottle designed as the last editions of the Opium collection. The bottle is dark and decorated with sequins that give a glam rock look.
</p>

<p></p>

<p>The face of the perfume's campaign is British model Edie Campbell, shot by Daniel Wolfe. Black Opium is available as 30, 50 and 100 ml Eau de Parfum.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2288492">lilysparfum</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-23"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729668635" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is very strong, very long lasting, has a great sillage. I loved this perfume when I was in high school, other people loved it too. However, now I seem to have grown out of my love for it. When I smell this, it smells like sickly sweet licorice. On my body it lacks any woodiness, any coffee notes. It is simply a flat sweet sugar perfume, which I find quite cloying throughout the day. It gives me a bit of a headache. I enjoy smelling it on other people, as it’s an inoffensive sweet fragrance, but I find it is actually quite offensive on me. I will say this perfume is very long lasting, as it lasts on clothes for over 24 hours, but in my case that is not a total positive.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; La cosa peggiore che ho letto è la confusione che qualcuno ha fatto tra black opium e opium ,una cosa direi oltraggiosa. Come si può confondere un capolavoro meraviglioso come Opium del 77 con questo intruglio chimico di frutta caffe cioccolato e patchouli che, per carità, si può indossare e amare, ma non è certo un profumo adulto e sensuale come il vero Opium.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I think I WOULD like a full bottle of this. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1974858">Pritsprits</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-09">10/09/24 11:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I feel like the marketing of this is almost a lie. I'm getting 0 coffee from this, and barely any vanilla whatsoever. It's funny how some people describe this as a gourmand fragrance, IT'S NOT.<br />
Does that make it a "bad" scent? Not at all! It's very pleasant in fact. A very nice blend of white florals with pear and patchouli in my opinion. I can definitely vision myself wearing this. <br />
<br />
The real problem I have with this is the longevity. I wore this on a very relaxed walk during fall weather and it had dissapeared within 2-3 hours max. Considering the price point that's very dissappointing . Especially considering this being advertised as a "night out" fragrance, this wouldn't survive going out before the night gets any interesting. You'd definitely have to reapply this a few times throughout the night!<br />
Make sure to get a sample of this before committing to a bottle!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2310174"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2310174#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2310068" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1287247">Strawberrythinking...</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 11:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I am leaving a new review of this fragrance, 5 years after my previous one. This was the first scent that I ever bought after I became interested in fragrances. Back then, I believed that the presence of vanilla in a fragrance automatically made it gourmand. I was looking for an edible vanilla coffee scent which I did not find with this, so it disappointed me. However, I recently decided to try it before selling my 5 year old bottle. I am not sure if the fragrance aged over time or if my taste did, but wow! Black Opium is a very jasmine-forward scent. It smells like creamy jasmine on my skin with a bit of vanilla and a whisper of coffee and pepper. It is "generic" maybe because it was so popular. I do smell it on people regularly. However, it smells expensive and can fit many occasions (especially a night out, though). Gives me a feeling of getting ready and wearing makeup, or maybe the smell of some high-end skincare. I'm starting to prefer it to my celebrity fragrances (besides Eilish No.1, that tops all).  It is a nice fragrance and I don't think I'm going to sell mine. I'll keep it for if I ever want a boost of jasmine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2295891"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2295891#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294678" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2008216">malebinha</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-14">09/14/24 13:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A saída floral branco e ardida soa clichê, mas esse floral logo evolui para um café amendoado, abaunilhado levemente amadeirado.<br />
<br />
É um perfume com baixíssima projeção, mas boa fixação, porém não tanto quanto gostaria.<br />
Nas roupas fixa de 6h à 10h.<br />
<br />
Ele cheira à Evanescence banda 😅 mulheres estilo emo entendem que o sombrio dessa fragrância é extremamente meigo. Um gourmand maduro, o que pode ser muito raro.<br />
Minha fragrância de clima frio, pois não agride ninguém.<br />
<br />
Um fato engraçado sobre quando conheci essa fragrância, lembro que era madrugada e senti um cheio de café sendo feito às 2h da manhã, pensei "quem é o viciado que acorda esse horário pra fazer café?" Tinha esquecido completamente que no meio dessa baunilha intimista, existia um café puro e aromático capaz de exalar tão natural.<br />
<br />
Quem acha um perfumo pouco elaborado, é porque claramente sente apenas a saída e a baunilha. Dê outra chance quando possível.<br />
Honestamente, só resenha perfumes que fiquei no mínimo alguns meses usando, pois as percepções mudam com o tempo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2282817"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2282817#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2282575" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is a warm, sweet and cozy scent albeit a bit on a heavy side. Coffee note is quite prominent and mixes deliciously with jasmine, pear and patchouli notes.<br />
<br />
Sadly for me, longevity is short, and to add more, it fades a bit into this cheap vanilla note. I do not know how to explain it, sometimes it resembles those tree shaped car air fresheners. That synthetic note might make this perfume smell cheap for other people. There is a similar note in YSL Libre perfume, too. Ignoring this note, it is quite good for a winter evening wear.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2276804"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2276804#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273827" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's not bad but it's definitely very far from groundbreaking. It's basic as hell. I'm 100% positive I've owned at least one REALLY cheap perfume that smelled exactly like this years ago. The worst part is I cannot smell the coffee note for the life of me, I swear it doesn't exist on my skin. Just vanilla mixed with something strong and I think sour? I would kill for a coffee or cacao scent (even more for a bloody fragrance because I'm anemic LOL but those are hard to find especially where I live so coffee it is).<br />
<br />
Spent €126 (read: massive amount of money, for a singular fragrance especially.. and a fucking generic OK smelling one at that) on this when I could've bought two Diorshow 5 Couleurs eyeshadow palettes instead. Fuck my stupid baka life or whatever Kafka said.<br />
<br />
All that being said as you can see this will become my signature (only until I use up the one that I own at the moment, amen) for now because it's my first ever expensive fragrance (congratu-fucking-lations to myself) and I'm in love with the bottle itself. I refuse to bring ugliness in my life when it is controllable and I can never find something that's good enough (mainly smell wise of fucking course but also obviously the bottle) at the drugstore/for a normal or cheap price so this will have to do.<br />
<br />
I would kill for cheap(er) Inexcusable Evil Toskovat' smellalikes, or at least ones that are available in (or surrounding) my country.<br />
<br />
EDIT (important ?) :<br />
Same day as initial thoughts/review --&gt; my brother also tried it (skin/wrist) and it smelled super vanilla and sweet on him with a hint of spice/sourness, while we both agreed that on me it smells extremely spicy with little to no sweetness.<br />
Three days later --&gt; I love it now. Lol. It's everything. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2248365" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MikoWhiffs"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1185991"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1185991.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MikoWhiffs" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2248365ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2248365" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1185991">MikoWhiffs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-13">08/13/24 17:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I first apply this fragrance, it’s so strong that I end up sneezing every time (I sprayed about 7 times on clothes and skin). Some people say it’s long-lasting, while others find it weak or just a skin scent. For me, it’s definitely weak. After about an hour, it fades so much that I can barely smell it unless I sniff really close. I even asked my friends to check if they could smell it on my clothes and wrist, and they all said it was very faint. It’s a great scent, but given the price and the lack of longevity, it just doesn’t seem worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2248365"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2248365#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2234467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2234467" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="hollykdenton"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1176787"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="hollykdenton" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Escada/Cherry-in-the-Air-17129.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.17129.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cherry in the Air"title="Cherry in the Air"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2234467ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2234467" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1176787">hollykdenton</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-31">07/31/24 03:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I collect Black Opium flankers, and the original is my least favourite of those that I own. That's not to say that I don't like it - I do, I just like the flankers better. The original EDP is a sweet white floral with vanilla and patchouli, and maybe just a hint of coffee. It's very well blended, but not as strong or long lasting as I'd like. I keep it mainly for comparison purposes.<br />
<br />
Keep reading if you're interested in how the flankers compare to the original.<br />
<br />
Extreme: similar to the original, but stronger, deeper and longer lasting. It has more patchouli, and is a little less sweet and a little less floral. The patchouli is quite prominent, but in a more gourmand way rather than being earthy or dirty. I can actually smell the coffee in this one! Or maybe it's the cacao. Either way, it's deep, rich and long lasting. I think of this as what the original should be (according to my taste for strong, heavy gourmand scents).<br />
<br />
Le Parfum: VANILLA. warm, sugary, caramel, and jasmine. The longest lasting vanilla I own, and one of the longest lasting BO flankers I have tried, along with Extreme. Despite the jasmine note, I kind of want to eat it. This might be my favourite of the bunch.<br />
<br />
Over Red: CHERRY VANILLA with a hint of green mandarin and tea. I smell white florals, but they seem different to me than the jasmine and orange blossom found in the other flankers. The cherry lasts throughout wearing, despite being a top note, although the overall longevity of this isn't huge, maybe 3-4 hours on me. It's a yummy, cozy scent.<br />
<br />
Neon: ORANGE BLOSSOM with a little bit of vanilla and jasmine, but no fruity/citrus notes unless they're just adding a bit of sweetness. I love it, but it sadly doesn't last long - I can detect no trace at all after 2-3 hours. My bottle is new, so it might improve over time.<br />
<br />
Illicit Green: I sampled this but didn't purchase as it is too similar to the original to my nose. I can smell the added fig and something a little bit fresh and green, but it's not different enough to warrant a spot in my collection.<br />
<br />
Intense: the black sheep of the family. The opening is quite heavy on the anise, which I don't mind, but I didn't purchase as I don't think I'd reach for it. I didn't detect any blackberry. It also had very poor longevity on my skin. Without the patchouli in the base, it faded away to an underwhelming, transparent vanilla licorice base within 30 minutes, and then to nothing at all within the hour.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2234320" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fr4grantk1tty&lt;3"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1773386"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1773386.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="fr4grantk1tty&lt;3" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2234320ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2234320" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1773386">fr4grantk1tty&lt;3</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-30">07/30/24 22:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>my signature scent!! the love of my life!! &lt;3<br />
<br />
this perfume is just everything i look for in a fragrance!! it is sweet, feminine, but also dark &amp; intoxicating. the opening pink pepper &amp; pear is such an intricate combination, alongside the soft white floral scent of orange blossom. the twinge of spice from the pink pepper complements the pear really nicely, but as the fragrance settles, the coffee and vanilla engulf the previous and surrounding notes in a beautiful, sexy mixture.<br />
<br />
to me, this perfume smells like a mysterious woman sitting alone on the stairs of her Victorian-style apartment, drinking an espresso martini while admiring the city lights in the foggy night, bundled up in her brown vintage fur coat. a divine woman who's kindness is of angels and who's eyes are full of twinkling stars (what i get from the vanilla &amp; white florals). but a woman who also values herself and her independence, would 100% mysteriously disappear into a foggy alleyway after classily turning down a degenerate trying to catcall her (what i get from the coffee, licorice, &amp; pink pepper). <br />
<br />
although i adore this perfume with all my heart, i do wish that it lasted a bit longer. i spray it twice on my neck, once on each wrist, and at first, the sillage is pretty strong so i wouldn't want to spray any more, because then it would be too daunting. However, the sillage dies down within 4-5 hours, leaving a very subtle trace, that i can barely smell, unless if i really sniff hard. but overall, i don't mind it that much since the fragrance is just sooooooo good!! <br />
<br />
generally speaking, black opium was love at first whiff for me. if i had to describe it using another analogy, the scent reminds me of depeche mode's music; the mysterious industrial instruments being the dark &amp; intoxicating coffee, licorice, pink pepper, &amp; almond, and Dave Gahan's beautiful, rich vocals, the vanilla and white floral notes. a beautiful orchestrated performance from all components, with a strong sweet characteristic that leaves an exquisite imprint.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2227069" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jellybear"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2124729"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jellybear" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2227069ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2227069" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2124729">Jellybear</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-23">07/23/24 10:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To my nose this is much more versatile than people give it credit for. For those who call it basic, I actually find this quite unique. We are in an era where all designer perfumes seem to share the same sparkling fruity floral DNA, but this to me is different. It's neither bright nor fresh. I imagine a luxurious continental breakfast at a very high end hotel, you can smell the coffee, some fresh fruits, an elegant bouquet is on the table. Yet, it has a mysterious and powerful edge to it. I agree with many others who have said it will shine in cold weather but I still think you can get away with it year round. It's signature worthy. It has a presence however. I personally would use caution wearing this in a professional office setting, but again, it's more versatile than people give it credit for, with a light hand it would still be fine. Overall I love it and I think it's iconic and classic for a reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2227069"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2227069#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2227043" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
And you know why? I think it’s because it’s just not me! So, the perfume isn’t bad, as it is just not my vibe. I think people need to learn the difference between a bad perfume and one that isn’t for them.<br />
<br />
I’m a fruity gourmand, or a ozonic fresh perfume type girly. <br />
<br />
I will have to revisit because, at the moment,  I just don’t enjoy this fragrance. Something about it is very smokey and sultry to me. It screams heavy and opulence. It’s that sexy girl, in a dark dimly-lit bar, with the jet black hair and ebony skin. The one oozing cool with a personality like Jessica Rabbit. Immaculate and suave. <br />
<br />
There is no sweet and light. It’s almost suffocating and stifling. Lilith personified. A witchy smell.<br />
<br />

I can see why people like it, but unfortunately, I’m not one of those girlies.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2226294"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2226294#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2225512" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s just not for me. It’s not bad …it’s pretty and I understand why it’s popular. There are no notes that truly stand out to my nose and on the other hand …the combo of all together does not blow me away either (which has happened with some other perfumes). It smells vaguely generic “perfumey”  on me. When I tried it in the Winter (cold) I didn’t really pick it up at all. So yep …not my jam. Oh well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2225512"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2225512#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2224837" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I smelled this way back our first date and IM HOOKED. It's warm, dark, and strong on the coffee and vanilla note. It reminds me of vanilla latte with the espresso made of robusta beans. If you're addicted to caffeine like me, it's a no-brainer that you will get addicted to this fragrance too. Be careful to blind buy cause it may not be everyone's cup of "coffee" *wink wink*</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2211554"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2211554#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2210510" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2210510" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ioniccolette"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1659539"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1659539.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ioniccolette" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2210510ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2210510" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1659539">ioniccolette</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-06">07/06/24 20:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was gifted this one for my birthday as a surprise. More surprisingly, I've found this one could be cousins with Giorgio Armani's Sì Intense. Both are wonderful winter scents with very similar profiles. Their differences lie in that Sì Intense is the currant-forward, 'flighty' younger cousin, and Black Opium is the coffee-forward, 'grounded' older cousin.<br />
<br />
Refocusing on Black Opium, though-- this one is incredibly warm and sultry. I'm genuinely surprised that there is patchouli in this one, and frankly ecstatic that it is never pronounced through the dry down. <br />
<br />
I honestly do not detect any of the top notes listed. For my nose, this one is a warm and sweetened coffee, almost chocolatey. It is a composition that starts dark and rich, like hiding in a coffee shop to escape the bitter cold in the evening. <br />
<br />
It surprisingly lightens to a more powdery profile as it develops, similar to finding out that in the back of the coffee shop is a little bakery. But there is never any impression of pear or orange blossom.<br />
<br />
As for the bottle, it's an interesting design, but it doesn't seem to match the composition or title. The glitter seems fitting for a 'bouncier' or 'flashier' kind of fragrance-- but this is just me. <br />
<br />
For the fragrance itself, Black Opium's quality impression is considerably highly dependent on the weather. I've found myself enjoying it only in the evenings, when I'm keeping to myself. <br />
<br />
When I was still getting acquainted with my gift, I tried it one balmy day, and it was far too loud. It chased me for the rest of that day. Definitely a fragrance that will wear you, if given the opportunity or right circumstances. <br />
<br />
Office-friendly? Perhaps. Maybe in the coldest months, it might get a free pass, as the sillage and longevity could be suppressed by the change of weather. The warmer months turn this one beastly.<br />
<br />
All in all, this one is perfect for colder evenings near the end or beginning of the year, and I'm personally looking forward to reaching for it in the upcoming winter mornings.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2175702" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="HYLAS"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453077"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1453077.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="HYLAS" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2175702ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2175702" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453077">HYLAS</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-02">06/02/24 10:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Black Opium screams pink candy, teeny locker room vibes and tooth rot! And that’s . . . kind of a compliment? Like, it’s kind of nostalgic? Kind of, She’s The One (Night Stand?).<br />
<br />
The only note I could accurately detect being the patchouli, it’s a bit of a sugar bomb, opening with a burst of candied fruit. The subtleties of pear and orange blossom were sadly lost on me. Over-sweet fairground vibes aplenty, a la JPG’s Scandal Le Parfum. But I gave it some grace, allowed it to dried down and, well, that sugar clung on like a free solo climber.<br />
<br />
In a nutshell, Black Opium gives me Jimmy Choo Flash meets Giorgio Armani Sì meets Valentino Donna Born In Roma. It’s a first date vibe. Young and sexy. Maybe a little insecure. Maybe nerves and butterflies. An underlying air of excitement. Then again, it also gives “I’m working late, ’cos I’m an exotic dancer”. Heads may turn . . . you may be remembered . . . for better or for worse!<br />
<br />
I don’t know. I’m torn. Without much of a sweet tooth, I may be a little biased. It’s kind of sexy. But maybe on someone else, not me. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1964083">karluvmost</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-11">05/11/24 09:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I like the smell of this perfume, but unfortunately, it is too strong for me. At first when I smelled it in the perfume shop, I was pleasantly surprised (I expected it to smell bad, I don't know why) by the smell, but after several hours, it got too overwhelming and intrusive. I don't know if it's the patchouli, most probably yes, but my head started to hurt from it. It's very strong and long lasting, which can be both good or bad depending if you like it or not. Overall, I like the smell, but I wish it wasn't this much "intoxicating".</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2152721"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2152721#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2151226" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2151226" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="parfumparfan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111549"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="parfumparfan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chloe/Cedrus-57246.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.57246.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cedrus"title="Cedrus"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2151226ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2151226" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111549">parfumparfan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-09">05/09/24 22:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Chances are you've probably smelled this before. It's ubiquitous and a consistent top-seller for good reason. However, that being said, I think it's been imitated too much or it was just not that ground-breaking when it came out. It reminds me of something from the Sol de Janeiro line (not the original Cheirosa '62) but something similar--sweet, edible, with just enough lotion floral on top. It's mass-market at its okay-est. It has decent staying power (6+ hours) but meh sillage on skin. I just don't think for the price or the meh performance or the ubiquity that you should actively look for it today. If you get it as a gift, hooray, use it for cooler temps and nighttime when you want an easy crowd-pleaser. But there are so many more interesting perfumes out there. It's a good fragrance but I don't know if it "did something" like the other ubiquitous fragrances of other eras (CK One, DKNY be delicious, l'eau d'issey, Angel, Coco Mademoiselle). It certainly didn't usher in any ground-breaking new compositions or anything, but it did define an era (at least for me). That being said, out of all the smell-alikes, this fragrance would be the winner because there are no sickening rose accords on top of all the gourmand notes. It's very balanced. If you like this you'd probably like Lancome's La Vie Est Belle, Viktor &amp; Rolf's Flowerbomb, Armani Code flankers Satin (true gourmand with praline) or Cashmere (reminds me of Hypnotic Poison with the almond/heliotrope going on), or for an underrated cheapie, Hanae Mori Hanae (pink bottle). It's a good one to have but not "run and get a bottle now!". <br />
6.8/10<br />
Edit:<br />
This has a delightful drydown. For whatever reason my skin amplifies woodsy notes above all else; once the floral-sweetness fades away, this leaves a really nice, cozy woods scent. I'd pick this over all its friends. <br />
8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2151226"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2151226#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2150757" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1762304">leahlowe02</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-08">05/08/24 06:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I received a miniature version of Black Opium with another YSL purchase. Black Opium's scent begins with a brisk night walk through a flower garden, dew clinging to leaves and air condensing as breath. Initially, I thought of the opening as too harsh and almost clinical, but patience is key, I suppose with all fragrances. It develops with time. The loudness of the pepper, pear and orange blossom notes die down after a few minutes with conservative application and notes of vanilla and jasmine emerge entwined with dewy florals. The coffee notes people have commented on is something I haven't been able to pick up on nor licorice -- I mainly get cold winter evening eating vanilla ice cream in a flower garden at midnight. Sileage is quite long lasting and projection I assume is pretty potent, given how little I needed to use to be hit with the scent. Overall, I would rate Black Opium a 7/10 - it's not quite me but I can appreciate what it's trying to be.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2149377"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2149377#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2148100" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; About 10 years ago I wanted this with a sore heart. There are better perfumes out there for the price point of this. Now I do like it, but all I get is florals and vanilla.  It doesn't last long which is disappointing.  I won't buy a full size bottle. It's a pretty scent, crowd pleaser,  if you like a soft vanilla you will like this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2148100"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2148100#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2148007" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2144440" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="molten_pearl"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1798388"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1798388.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="molten_pearl" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2144440ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2144440" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1798388">molten_pearl</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-03">05/03/24 09:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Black Opium was the first fragrance I had ever obsessed over. I sampled it once at a department store and was convinced, at the ripe age of 15, that this would be my signature scent. I told myself that once I finally had enough money, I'd buy myself a bottle. Flash forward to my 16th birthday and my lovely friends had bought me a 10 ml travel sized rollerball of this stuff. I was over the moon. <br />
<br />
Its been years since then, and the 10 ml rollerball remains largely untouched. Somewhere along my journey into womanhood, the scent became too sweet, too cloying, and too headache inducing. Every time I wear it, I feel like a fourth-grader sneaking into her teenage sisters room and trying on her stuff. <br />
<br />
The scent itself is vaguely sugary and floral. It takes effort to actually smell the coffee, but once you do, you're reminded of an overly sweet Frappuccino you ordered as a pre-teen because that's what all the cool girls drank and you didn't know enough about coffee to know any better. I've smelt it on the subway a thousand times before and I'll likely keep smelling it for years to come. <br />
<br />
Performance is nothing to write home about.<br />
<br />
Its a nice scent, don't get me wrong. But I'm over it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2144440"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2144440#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2141952" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I also get lavender/vetiver. The coffee is discreet initially but comes forward a bit more in dry-down like roasted coffee and combined with the orange blossom and fruitiness gives a bitter-warm touch.<br />
<br />
Zara's "Gardenia"(the newest version) is similar but has less coffee, lacks licorice/almond, has amberwood and a bit more vanilla. Gardenia is fine but I'd opt for Black Opium as it's more complex, refined and smooth - just beautiful.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2136079"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2136079#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2135846" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Without a care in the world, I found myself in a luxurious department store, where I liberally spritzed this perfume onto the coat I wore every chilly night of the trip. Upon returning home, I promptly acquired a full-size bottle to cherish.<br />
<br />
Over the years, I've transformed into a completely different woman. My life and values have taken a 180-degree turn, and I couldn't be happier. I've let go of most things, connections, and perfumes that remind me of the past, but this one has remained in my collection.<br />
<br />
Although I'll never purchase another cloyingly sweet perfume, this one has a little more character to it, and I eagerly anticipate winter nights to savor it. Despite my aversion to fruity and overly sweet scents, I can appreciate its well-blended composition and unique character, even if it's somewhat questionable. It's like that one popular, obnoxious girl in high school who everyone secretly, or not so secretly, despises but can't deny her authenticity.<br />
<br />
Safe Blind Buy: Yes, If you like sweet designer fragrance.   <br />
Presentation: 8/10  <br />
Longevity &amp; Projection: Moderate.<br />
<br />
May peace be upon you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2133784"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2133784#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2133704" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

I don't get anything spicier than a hint of cinnamon, but this also doesn't come across as synthetic or cloying, which is what I'm trying to avoid when I look for sweet scents blended with pepper. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/886089">wildangel72</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-24">03/24/24 03:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The bad rap this scent gets is overblown and undeserved imo.  I'm sure some ppl genuinely don't like it, nothing works for everybody, but once 1 or 2 influencers on social media slammed Black Opium using words like cheap, granny, wannabe, and even "cringe" the easily influenced masses just piled on.  Even if it's not your style or doesn't work with your chemistry, this scent is in no way "trashy" or old lady, and liking it does not make you "basic" (Anna Bey 🙄🙄).  It's a great balance of sweet and musky/spicy that keeps it from leaning too gourmand, and it's one of the scents in my huge collection that I get the most compliments on.  The Nuit Blanche flanker was even better, and I'm so sad it was discontinued.  I have a little of that one left, and I'll continue buying the original.  Try it for yourself and if you don't like it, fine, but don't dismiss it out of hand and potentially miss out on a great addition to your scent wardrobe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1817602">dickhard</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-11">02/11/24 07:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The first perfume I was ever addicted to. I remember spraying a tester strip at Ulta with my mom when I was in high school, putting in my pocket and completely forgetting about it, then a couple hours later frantically searching my jacket to find whatever smelled so fucking good. I remember thinking how expensive of a purchase it was for me at the time ($80 to a high schooler). It felt like it marked a transition to adulthood. I sprayed it liberally, which I now cringe to think about, because the scent is so strong and clubby and sex-juicy, and I was wearing it to work as a tutor. That being said, it did smell good on my skin. The notes mixed in a magical way, I got very heavy coffee and vanilla with something a little bite-y. From 18-23 this was my signature scent, which honestly seems like the point of this fragrance. It's perfect for young hot girls. My friends and I all shared it. We'd suffocate anyone in the car with us on the way to the bar. It's seductive, youthful, trashy, destructive.<br />
<br />
I bought a bottle last Christmas for nostalgia purposes after a couple years and resold it after one spray. The love affair was over. I outgrew it, which I think is also the point of fragrances, sometimes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="2058959"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=2058959#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="25324" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1209292" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="KittyDeBeauvoir"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1212801"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1212801.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="KittyDeBeauvoir" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Dolce-Gabbana-Pour-Femme-15335.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.15335.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dolce&Gabbana Pour Femme"title="Dolce&Gabbana Pour Femme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1209292ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1209292" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1212801">KittyDeBeauvoir</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-08-09">08/09/20 04:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me start off by saying I am way late for the "Black Opium" train. <br />
I didn't buy a bottle of this earlier on for...some unknown reason. <br />
<br />
Sweet baby Jesus - this is delicious!<br />
It helps that coffee is my addiction of choice, and one I don't intend to follow any 12-Step program to overcome.<br />
<br />
On first spray, you get a tiny bit of fresh pear. It's really very sweet and uplifting - similar to the original "Jimmy Choo" without the patchouli mixed way up in there.<br />
<br />
Then - coffee and vanilla! <br />
Ooooh growling Mama-Bears, this is intoxicating and sweet. It is one of the better examples of a warm gourmand we have out there.<br />
I honestly don't get a lot of any of the white florals. Can't really detect jasmine or orange blossom at any time, but honestly - they're not needed.<br />
<br />
This is perfect for winter and autumn. It's SO COZY! Hence, it's incredible appeal for colder weather. As for being a night-fragrance? Nah, I spray this any typical day, and I don't fuss.<br />
<br />
IMPORTANT TO NOTE: This is not restricted to *any* age. I often smell this on my 70-ish-year-old colleague - and I LOVE IT ON HER! She smells so incredible with this on. I tend to immediately stop in my tracks, turn around, stalk straight back on up to her, and demand that she confirm my olfactory suspicions that this is "Black Opium". Thankfully, she finds me charming. If not a little creepy.<br />
If anyone tells you this is for teenagers and 20-somethings only, tell them to walk their poor-smelling selves back to the office of "Convenient Theories For You Daily", and sign up for a subscription.<br />
Don't give me that rubbish.<br />
<br />
The downside, folks - The sillage is enchanting (read above), yet variable on folks. Great on my colleague; relatively decent on me. The longevity is...almost universally poor. It takes great restraint on my part not to spray myself 8-10 times a day.<br />
<br />
The bottle? *chef's kiss*<br />
<br />
***<br />
<br />
Kitty rating: 8.5/10<br />
<br />
~Compliment Counter~: 2 compliments 😁😁</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25324"comment_id="1209292"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Black-Opium-25324.html?ccid=1209292#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="25324" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

<br />
Anyway, I have to admit that the coffee note is intriguing, but - in reality - it really doesn't translate into anything that would warrant the purchase based on that "unique factor" alone. <br />
<br />
On reflection I think that, maybe, it's the powerful sweetness that is just too much for me - or perhaps it's more than that, I'm not sure. In any case I'd classify this one as a try-hard fragrance: she thinks that she's projecting a bad girl vibe, but all I'm reading is "basic"!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
